[30;1m1161 | [0m[35m  performance, it has been removed (from Chris McDonough).[0m
[30;1m1162 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m506 | [0m[35m* Request objects now accept an additional constructor parameter:[0m
[30;1m507 | [0m[35m  ``url_encoding``.  ``url_encoding`` will be used to decode PATH_INFO and[0m

[30;1m510 | [0m[35m  constructor, the default value ``utf-8`` will be used to decode the[0m
[30;1m511 | [0m[35m  PATH_INFO and SCRIPT_NAME.[0m
